  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer4380348602539424773">You’re not supposed to want the one who torments you. <br/><br/>When my stepbrother, Elec, came to live with us my senior year, I wasn’t prepared for how much of a jerk he’d be. <br/><br/>I hated that he took it out on me because he didn’t want to be here. <br/>I hated that he brought girls from our high school back to his room. <br/>But what I hated the most was the unwanted way my body reacted to him</span>
  <span id="freeText4380348602539424773" style="display:none">You’re not supposed to want the one who torments you. <br /><br />When my stepbrother, Elec, came to live with us my senior year, I wasn’t prepared for how much of a jerk he’d be. <br /><br />I hated that he took it out on me because he didn’t want to be here. <br />I hated that he brought girls from our high school back to his room. <br />But what I hated the most was the unwanted way my body reacted to him. <br /><br />At first, I thought all he had going for him were his rock-hard tattooed abs and chiseled face. Then, things started changing between us, and it all came to a head one night. <br /><br />Just as quickly as he’d come into my life, he was gone back to California. <br /><br />It had been years since I’d seen Elec. <br /><br />When tragedy struck our family, I’d have to face him again. <br /><br />And holy hell, the teenager who made me crazy was now a man that drove me insane.<br /><br />I had a feeling my heart was about to get broken again.<br /><br />Stepbrother Dearest is a standalone novel. <br /><br />**Contains graphic sexual content and harsh language. It is only appropriate for adult readers age 18+</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062507833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16302764121794481008">So... <br/>Where to start? <br/><br/>I am always intrigued with books dealing with taboo topics (or in this case pseudo-taboo), especially incestuous relationships. At first I crossed this book from my TBR shelf because it seemed like a trashy romance. But then all this five stars reviews started popping out all over the Goodreads. So, I gave in to the temptation. And once again, I should have stick to the original plan. <br/><br/><b>The story.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404311985ra/10223423.gif' width='497' height='263' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The horror! My eyes!!! What is this shit???<br/><br/>But seriously, if you are getting off</span>
  <span id="freeText16302764121794481008" style="display:none">So... <br>Where to start? <br><br>I am always intrigued with books dealing with taboo topics (or in this case pseudo-taboo), especially incestuous relationships. At first I crossed this book from my TBR shelf because it seemed like a trashy romance. But then all this five stars reviews started popping out all over the Goodreads. So, I gave in to the temptation. And once again, I should have stick to the original plan. <br><br><b>The story.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404311985ra/10223423.gif" width="497" height="263" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The horror! My eyes!!! What is this shit???<br><br>But seriously, if you are getting off on forbidden sexual relationships, read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2741079.Selena_Kitt" title="Selena Kitt" rel="nofollow noopener">Selena Kitt</a>. At least you know what you are about to get when you pick up her novels - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5982208.Naughty_Bits" title="Naughty Bits by Selena Kitt" rel="nofollow noopener">Naughty Bits</a> is a hard core brother/sister erotica. For those who are a bit squeamish, there is even a bit tamer version of the same story - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18394981.Yank" title="Yank by Selena Kitt" rel="nofollow noopener">Yank</a>. <br><br>Back to <i>Stepbrother Dearest</i>. The only selling point of this book is forbidden romance. I believe that it was what appealed to the most of the girls who were all moon eyed after finishing this book. <br>Story is divided in two parts - first is about how they met when they were 17 and second is taking place seven years later. <br><br><b>What happens?</b> They meet, they lust, they fight, they hang out, they fight, play video games, go out on double date, fight, lust,kiss, he treats like she is worthless, she cries, they lust again, fight again, and - epic finale, they fuck. He is whore, she is virgin. She is "clean" like flower in pretty meadow, and all other girls are worthless sluts. <br><br>She is idiot who lets him treat her like a trash. <br>He is a jerk/bad boy/lost soul/little boy in hot, pierced, tattooed body.<br><br>Whole book is series of their "forbidden encounters" and fighting against what they feel. <u>No character development. No. Plot. Development.</u> <br>How was this written? <i>Oh look, girls like to read about bad boys, let's put that in. What does it mean to be a bad boy? A lot of tattoos, pierced lip, pierced dick, he should be moody and grunt a lot. He is so hot that all girls throw themselves at him - so he fucks a lot. But, he needs to have some signature move - he can't fuck like a regular person. He has to be a bit rough and crude. Oh, I know - let him have fixation with necks. Like, biting them. Or maybe even strangling them lightly. Yeah, that would work. But he is not actually bad. He has daddy issues. Mommy is crazy like a bat. He is really a little boy who wants to be loved.But that is not enough. We need more drama. Because girls love drama! Oh, I know! Spanish soap operas, thank you for this brilliant idea. <br>"I am my brother's bastard son." <br>Yes, that would be so awesome. His parents were in forbidden relationship. Just like he wants to be with his stepsister. Ugh, wait... No just like that. His brother is not his father. Their father is their father. His brother is his stepfather. But his mommy never loved his father. He was... But his brother hates him. He verbally abuses him. His mother is depressed. She is artist. He is wannabe writer. He is not a bad boy. He just looks like one. Because he has daddy/brother/mommy issues.<br><br>Now what about girl? Of course she has to virgin, because she is a good girl. But she is not naive - she has vibrator. She is super polite and good. And she constantly repeats how her stepbrother is hot and imagines hundred dirty things she would like to do to him. He treats her like she's worthless, but that won't make her give up on him because she sees how vulnerable and good underneath he is. How? Meh.. that doesn't matter - only important thing are her nipples. Yes, she should have sensitive nipples. <br><br>The most important thing - a lot of make out and almost make out scenes.<br><br>Oh, and in the part 2 there will me everything from the part 1 told from his point of view. Word for word, in case people missed anything. So they can read it. All over again.</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394998207ra/8933593.gif" width="500" height="235" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I will repeat - if you are getting off on this kind of thing - read Selena Kitt. <br><br>I'm out! <br><br></span>

</a><br/><b>★★★★ ½! Stepbrother Dearest (stand-alone). Tragedy re-connects girl with the step-brother she still loves, but can’t have! Stepbrother Dearest = Heart Be Desert Ports!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I want to be the first one to show you everything and to be the one you’ll always remember for the rest of your life.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>Stepbrother Dearest</b> (stand-alone) opens up to high school senior <b>Greta Hansen</b> waiting for her stepbrother to arrive for a year-long stay. Nothing could have prepared her for <b>Elec</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5933924263665065713" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/WardStepbrotherdearestTiitebySueBee_zps5c6caa82.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/SBDcoverxBTbysb_zps95b88030.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413185955ra/11476436.gif" alt=" photo SBDcoverxBTbysb_zps95b88030.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413185955ra/11476437.gif" alt=" photo SBDstoryxBbysb_zpsf206e995.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★ ½! Stepbrother Dearest (stand-alone). Tragedy re-connects girl with the step-brother she still loves, but can’t have! Stepbrother Dearest = Heart Be Desert Ports!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I want to be the first one to show you everything and to be the one you’ll always remember for the rest of your life.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Stepbrother Dearest</b> (stand-alone) opens up to high school senior <b>Greta Hansen</b> waiting for her stepbrother to arrive for a year-long stay. Nothing could have prepared her for <b>Elec O’Rourke</b>. He is eerily handsome borderline beautiful, but he is also angry, broken, cocky and oh so determined not to like her. <b>Greta is smitten</b>, but in all her innocence doesn’t quite know how to deal with him. <br><br><b>
  <i>The sexual tension is off-the-charts…</i>
</b><br><br>Soon Greta starts getting <b>mixed signals from Elec</b>. <b>He taunts her</b> with his sexuality and his many girlfriends only to do or say something kind and then back to being hostile. In weak moments there are <b>stolen kisses</b> and <b>sexually charged conversations</b> with Greta hoping for more…<br><br><b>
  <i>Then Elec has to leave abruptly…</i>
</b><br><br>But not before <b>stealing Greta’s heart</b> and <b>accepting her innocence</b>. Some truths are revealed but for most parts Elec remains an enigma.<br><br><b>
  <i>Fast forward seven long years…</i>
</b><br><br>In many ways <b>Greta’s life stopped that fateful day</b>. Sure she went onto College, graduated, moved to New York and got a clerical job. She even had a brief engagement. But her heart never got over Elec. <b>She has cocooned herself in a mundane existence.</b><br><br>When <b>tragedy brings them together it’s a shock for both</b>. Everything has changed yet somehow it's just the way they left off. They still have this <b>intense, undeniable pull towards each other with too much standing in their way</b>. Elec remains elusive sending Greta mixed signals.<br><br>Much of story is them <b>navigating after tragedy</b>, spending time catching up and slowly <b>opening up</b> about their current and past situations. It’s a slow, painful process of uncovering <b>heartaches</b>; unimaginable <b>secrets</b> and <b>pains</b>. It’s also about <b>could-have-beens</b>, <b>regrets</b> and <b>hopelessness</b>. Ultimately it’s their story of an <b>soul searching passion</b> and <b>unending love</b> and how in life sometimes everything still isn’t enough….<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You were the best thing that ever happened to me. I hope someday I can say you were one of the best, but for now, it’s only you.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/SBDHBSbysb_zps1389377c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413185955ra/11476438.gif" alt=" photo SBDHBSbysb_zps1389377c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Eight words to describe <b>Elec O’Rourke: Captivating, broken, cocky, vulnerable, torn, observant, complex and secretive</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Holy hell… his tip was pierced. What a way to be introduced to my first live one.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/SBDheBSbysb_zps78995cb8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413185955ra/11476439.gif" alt=" photo SBDheBSbysb_zps78995cb8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Seven words to describe <b>Greta Hansen: Sweet, timid, unassuming, loyal, innocent, endearing and naive</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Physically, he was my dream and in every other way, my nightmare.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Stepbrother Dearest</b> is a <b>beautifully told tale</b>, a roller-coaster of events and emotions. At times painful to read. There are a couple of reason for book title with which will be revealed by the ending! My favorite was the first part and the young Elec. Overall I enjoyed their journey, but most <b>I loved where it left them!</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>The perfect ending = Rec Penned Gift!</i>
</b><br><br><b>Excellent</b> story-telling! <b>Angsty</b> and <b>engaging</b> plot! <b>Swoon-worthy</b> hero! <i>Just like Elec kept a piece of Greta’s heart, he kept part of mine.</i><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He kept his hand on my throat and lightly squeezed it. It was innocent, but there was a fine line being drawn with every second that passed.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars then 4 stars<br>Heroine rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sexual tension rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4 stars<br>Plot rating: 4 stars<br>Dialogue rating: 4.5 stars<br>Storytelling rating: 4.5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 5 stars<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br>*********************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4.5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this book: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20for%20my%20reads/SBDrevendxBbysb_zps3f13e46a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer16926954118993233205"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 stars!! ::: </b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412102401i/11324308.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>WOW!! I was hooked on this book from the moment I started it and I could not put it down until the end!! An angsty, unconventional love story and such a roller coaster! It was absolutely unputdownable.<br/><br/>When Greta's stepbrother came to live with them during her senior year, she never expected him to be such a jerk, and she certainly never expected to feel so drawn to him. He was stunning. Gorgeous. Hot. Tattooed and pierced (yes, there!!) with bad ha</span>
  <span id="freeText16926954118993233205" style="display:none"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 stars!! ::: </b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412102401i/11324308.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WOW!! I was hooked on this book from the moment I started it and I could not put it down until the end!! An angsty, unconventional love story and such a roller coaster! It was absolutely unputdownable.<br><br>When Greta's stepbrother came to live with them during her senior year, she never expected him to be such a jerk, and she certainly never expected to feel so drawn to him. He was stunning. Gorgeous. Hot. Tattooed and pierced (yes, there!!) with bad habits and a bad attitude to match. And yet she sensed something behind his abrasive behaviour... something that showed her a vulnerability and hurt that she could see was eating away at him, and she was determined to get through to him one way or another. <br><br>He was rude, he lashed out with his words, paraded girls in front of her, and toyed with her emotions... and yet the next moment he was putting himself in harms way to protect her. One thing was certain: there was more to Elec than met the eye. <br><br>Once they got past their initial differences, he made it still clear that there were some lines he would not cross. And once she got to know him it became clear that underneath all the anger that he showed the world was a guy with a very good heart who wanted her just as much as she wanted him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You're the only girl in the entire world that's forbidden, and fuck me if that doesn't make me want you more than anything." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>But just when things were looking up, one night and one phone call changed everything. Forever. And just as quickly as he entered her life, he was gone again. And she didn't see him again for seven years.<br><br>When a family tragedy brought them both back home, they were both shocked to see how some things (heartbreaking things) had changed so much and others hadn't changed even one bit. <br><br>This is a sexy, angst-filled story of first love and forbidden desires. It's a story with imperfect people who sometimes choose wrong. It's a story with heart break and angst, but also with healing and growth. And most of all it's a story of learning to follow your heart. Sometimes, you just have to listen to your heart. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want to be the only one to show you everything and to be the one you'll always remember for the rest of your life." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Oh my gosh, their reunion just punched me in the gut. Again. And again. And again. That little twist. My poor heart was just shredded. But at the same time, I understood what had happened. It made sense given the timeline... but it didn't make it one but easier to read. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I know I'm not supposed to care. But when it comes to you, what I'm supposed to be feeling has never seemed to matter." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>There are no good stopping points in this book and it keeps you desperate to find out what happens next. But especially from about 54% on til the end, I'm pretty sure I didn't move once from my spot on the couch and just sat there madly flipping pages and devouring the story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'm... fighting the urge to back you up against this wall and fuck you so hard that I'll have to carry you back to your room." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>This is the kind of book where, once you start reading, you'll want to cancel all your plans for the rest of the day so that you can just keep reading it. I loved the way the author incorporated both sides of the story. It was a very unique way to show the dual POV and I thought it really worked well for this. There was so much that I loved about the story but it also wasn't perfect for me. There were some things (in the second half) that I might have wanted a little differently but they didn't stop me from loving the story and there's really no doubt that this book was completely unputdownable!!<br><br>If you want a sexy, unique, unconventional romance to fall in love with, try this one!!<br><br><b>Rating: 4.5 stars. Standalone New Adult Romance.</b><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<div id="review_1011788170" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1011788170" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1011788170?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1011788170" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2793822217268477825"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/b2ec69bf-203b-45ac-bcf4-e8c7fd218f36_zps6f871f04.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412759761i/11418638.jpg' alt=' photo b2ec69bf-203b-45ac-bcf4-e8c7fd218f36_zps6f871f04.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I’m not going to lie… the title and the cover of this book drew me right in and made me one click the minute it went live. I’ve never read this author and I wasn’t sure what the book was about (besides a stepbrother/stepsister) but I knew I had to read it. I LOVE forbidden love stories so the title alone drew me in. <i>Stepbrother Dearest</i> was different that I expected. It was a little ‘young’ for a lack of a better word, at the beginning. Then it got a little sweet and sexy. The last h</span>
  <span id="freeText2793822217268477825" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/b2ec69bf-203b-45ac-bcf4-e8c7fd218f36_zps6f871f04.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412759761i/11418638.jpg" alt=" photo b2ec69bf-203b-45ac-bcf4-e8c7fd218f36_zps6f871f04.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m not going to lie… the title and the cover of this book drew me right in and made me one click the minute it went live. I’ve never read this author and I wasn’t sure what the book was about (besides a stepbrother/stepsister) but I knew I had to read it. I LOVE forbidden love stories so the title alone drew me in. <i>Stepbrother Dearest</i> was different that I expected. It was a little ‘young’ for a lack of a better word, at the beginning. Then it got a little sweet and sexy. The last half was much more angsty. It was one of those books that wasn’t perfect for me, but it was also one that I read in one sitting so you know I was hooked from the start. <br><br>Greta’s stepbrother Elec is 17, just like her. She’s never met him, but he’s coming to stay with her family for a year while his mom travels from work. Greta wants to get to know Elec, to make him feel comfortable. Once she sees him, she is floored. He might be the most attractive guy she's met… but he’s also a jerk to her. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e90bc143-dd11-4d96-93cc-3d1f1429a351_zps65be401a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412759761i/11418639.jpg" alt=" photo e90bc143-dd11-4d96-93cc-3d1f1429a351_zps65be401a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Elec has a bad relationship with his father. He does not want to be living in that house, but doesn’t have much of a choice. Elec makes it his mission to give Greta a hard time. The harder he pushes, the more she tries to befriend him and get to know him. Slowly, she works her way in. <br><br>Elec and Greta have a unique relationship when they are teenagers. They’re only together a short time, but they start to become friends. As their friendship progresses, they find it hard to deny their obvious attraction to one another. Though they are together months, one night is all they really get together. One night of memories.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I’d rather have one night with you than nothing at all.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/6a3314ca-194b-4276-bd91-e2b99e60dce2_zps8559f01f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412759761i/11418640.jpg" alt=" photo 6a3314ca-194b-4276-bd91-e2b99e60dce2_zps8559f01f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Just know that I would stay with you if I could.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Elec can’t stay. He has other family issues that keep him away. And he stays away. For seven years. Seven years later, Greta is living in NYC. After a failed engagement, she is single and working. She’s content with her life. Then she gets a call from her mother that will change everything. It’s the call that brings Elec back into her life. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>The ‘one that got away’ was supposed to stay away, not come back and leave you all over again.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> Oh the emotions when Elec was back. I didn’t know what to feel. I know as I read and the more I learned of their situation, I bit my nails right to the quick. My heart was slowly breaking. The angst about killed me. No matter whats going on in their lives, Elec and Greta can’t deny the feelings they still have for one another. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I know I’m not supposed to care. But when it comes to you, what I’m supposed to be feeling has never seemed to matter.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>When reading a book, there are certain lines that just pop out at you. When I read this one, it brought me to tears. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/fad9e0eb-6d62-4ca6-a06a-c74a8f99930e_zps6de234ce.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412759761i/11418641.jpg" alt=" photo fad9e0eb-6d62-4ca6-a06a-c74a8f99930e_zps6de234ce.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There was a lot that I liked about this book. I liked both Elec and Greta. Both had moments where I wanted to shake them, but by the end of the book, I loved them both. I loved how the book ended. The beginning banter between Elec and Greta was great. There was a lot in the middle that stressed me out, but when I’m reading, I love when I get invested and feel like that, so it worked for me. <br><br>The main thing I can think of that would have made this book so much better for me is the last 30% or so from Elec’s perspective. Don’t get me wrong- I loved being in his head and I think it was really important to get his side of the story, but to basically re-tell from his perspective that late in the book was a miss for me. I wish that it would have been in dual pov and woven in that way. I understand why the author did it this way <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I’m sure it was because it he was following his dream as a writer and it was a big gesture to let her read his work and show his past and feelings that way <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, it just didn’t quite work for me.<br><br>Overall, I did enjoy this one a lot. It was a forbidden love story, but not in the way you would think. The fact that the two were step siblings wasn’t a huge forbidden issue, it was something else. If you’re looking for an angst-filled read with a decent amount of steam, some romance and a jerky and damaged book boyfriend who has a good heart, pick this one up! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/abd294c0-7c7c-4157-be25-5ad2f9652f00_zpsed8389ef.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412759761i/11418642.jpg" alt=" photo abd294c0-7c7c-4157-be25-5ad2f9652f00_zpsed8389ef.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2793822217268477825" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1012208931" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1012208931" />
    <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie"><img alt="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505392311p2/11641363.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1012208931?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=it-hurts-in-my-heart">it-hurts-in-my-heart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=talk-dirty-to-me">talk-dirty-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=bloody-love-triangle">bloody-love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=its-funny-ahahaha">its-funny-ahahaha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1012208931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2796101511825237835"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411671888i/11263681.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"You make me feel things, Greta. You always have. When I'm around you, whether it's good or bad...I feel everything.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Stepbrother Dearest, is written in two parts. In the first part the character are 17/18 years old and in highschool. In the second part the book fast forwards seven years. The characters are reunited, and so the story continues.<br/><br/>So first of all let me just say that, Stepbrother Dearest was a really great book. The writing was engaging, the characters multifaceted and th</span>
  <span id="freeText2796101511825237835" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411671888i/11263681.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"You make me feel things, Greta. You always have. When I'm around you, whether it's good or bad...I feel everything.</i>
</b><br><br>Stepbrother Dearest, is written in two parts. In the first part the character are 17/18 years old and in highschool. In the second part the book fast forwards seven years. The characters are reunited, and so the story continues.<br><br>So first of all let me just say that, Stepbrother Dearest was a really great book. The writing was engaging, the characters multifaceted and the pacing was pretty good too.<br><br>Secondly, 3.5 Stars is not a bad rating. It means as per Goodreads rating system that I liked the book bordering on really liked it.<br><br>Here's a quick summary of my feelings towards Stepbrother Dearest:<br>Yes, the story follows the relationship of Greta and Elec who are step-siblings. Elec's father married Greta's mother, and when Elec's mother gets a job opportunity overseas, she sends him to go live with his father and new wife and step daughter.<br><br>Here's where the story fell a bit flat for me. That first meeting between Elec and Greta was awesome, the sexual tension was palpable and the forbidden factor was pretty obvious and made the scene very enjoyable but unfortunately we had one POV and it was Greta's. So I was constantly reading about her lust and growing love for Elec, while I could pick up on Elec's growing attraction to Greta, it lacked intensity. Which is why I need his POV. I love a cocky alpha male, and I love it when he's so into the heroine his knee jerk reaction is to be mean. But I need his POV to counteract the meaness, otherwise I just think he's being a dick.<br><br><i>
  <b>That was the problem. I'd grown to love a little mean mixed in with my nice.</b>
</i> <br><br><b>Seven years</b><br>The characters are estranged for seven years, and when tragedy befalls the family, they're are reunited. The tension and angst was so obvious, and with both characters having moved on, mainly Elec who now had a girlfriend, it was pretty painful.<br><br>Here's where I get a bit ranty. Rants are not done because we want to slam the book, I just rant because I have all these emotions inside me that need to be let out.<br><br>Greta, was obviously still in love with Elec and I'm not sure but I think he was too, or maybe it was just lust. I don't know. I needed his POV, because quite honestly I started hating the guy. He had another girlfriend who he vocalised his love for at any given moment in front of Greta.<br><br>I'm sorry, Elec but don't I remember you saying you would never hurt her? And don't act dumb, you know she still has feelings for you!<br><br>So I regret to say the story became some sort of love triangle and you know what that's okay. But at least have the third party play an active role in the book, Chelsea was like a shield for Elec, he mentioned her when things got intense. Which was like a bucket of ice cold water to Greta.<br><br>And then lastly "the book", so I'm just going to spoiler tag this one.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Elec wrote a book. The book was Elec's POV, it was like a repeat of the entire book but from his perspective. Which quite honestly felt like a waste of time. His POV should have been interwoven into the book, it would have given me the reader the opportunity to empathise with Elec and not feel like he didn't want Greta as much as she wanted him. What annoyed me even more was the fact that he loved Chelsea, I mean he loved her a lot! But he loved Greta more. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And when the characters resolved their issues, Elec immediately wants to have kinky sex with Greta. And like the lovesick puppy she was she agreed. No, no and no. Firstly, Elec needed to do a lot more groveling. Elec ended up seeming like a spoiled brat who got everything he wanted and Greta ended up looking like a doormat. You have to make him work for it, girl!<br><br><i>
  <b>"Nothing says I'm sorry like a dick and a smile."</b>
</i><br><br>So by the end of the book I surmised that, Elec loved Greta first, but he also loved Chelsea. So unfortunately the book missed that 5 star mark for me.<br><br>P.S. It didn't really feel forbidden to me.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I've never got over hurting you the first time, but hurting you twice...believe me when I say this was the last thing I ever wanted to see happen in my life time.</i>
</b><br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by author in return for an honest review</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1019926835" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8416751203252561439"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412247451ra/11344313.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To tell you the truth, I was not going to write a review for this book, because I really don’t have anything positive to say about it. There are many things that are wrong with this book, but I’ll just address two.<br/><br/>First would be <b>the writing</b>. It was <b>juvenile</b>! Especially in the first part. The plot was repetitive: they flirt, they fight, he insults her, she runs to him like a love-struck puppy. This book was trite, cliché and juvenile. Did I already say that? Ah, I don’t care, because this book ob</span>
  <span id="freeText8416751203252561439" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412247451ra/11344313.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To tell you the truth, I was not going to write a review for this book, because I really don’t have anything positive to say about it. There are many things that are wrong with this book, but I’ll just address two.<br><br>First would be <b>the writing</b>. It was <b>juvenile</b>! Especially in the first part. The plot was repetitive: they flirt, they fight, he insults her, she runs to him like a love-struck puppy. This book was trite, cliché and juvenile. Did I already say that? Ah, I don’t care, because this book obviously doesn’t have a problem with repeating itself. What was that with Elec’s book? Repeating <u>exactly the same events</u> from his POV is so not cool. Dear author, that’s just plain cheating.<br> Overall, Stepbrother Dearest is a poorly written novel, IMO. <br><br>Second issue would be the main female protagonist – <b>Greta.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412247557ra/11344333.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The best thing Elec said to Greta in this entire novel is: <b>
  <u>Have some self-respect!</u>
</b> AMEN. Why didn’t you take that advice, told him to go screw himself and grow some big girl pants?<br><br>It really made me sad, the way she let him continually disrespect her. And I’m not even talking about the first part when they were teenagers. That was child’s play. I know how when you’re in love, you’re willing to forgive almost anything, but this. Here. Is. Not. Okay. This novel is not a true, healthy representative of what a normal relationship should be like. I mean, in the first part I was willing to forgive her, she’s young and in love. But then came that part <u>7 years after</u> and I was waiting to see the strong, independent woman she’s become. But, apparently she doesn’t exist. She’s still pinning after that jerk and lets him walk all over her. <br><br>Also, all these five-star reviews are pissing me off. I’ve scrolled though some of them and people who disliked the book gave it 3 stars. Wut? Folks, it’s okay to give 1 or 2 star ratings from time to time. It’s making me sad that some really amazing books are not getting enough attention while crap like this gets a lot of undeserved hype. <br><br>So, to conclude, I didn’t like it and don’t recommend it to anyone. <br><br>Over and out. <br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1041409615" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14461900067210588396">I loved this book! I had expected the story to be kind of hard to get into after reading many reviews that said it got off to a slow start. That was not my experience at all. The story of Elec and Greta captivated me from page one. I devoured this book!<br/><br/>Elec and Greta's story was full of passion, forbidden desire and angst. Reading their story took me on an emotional roller coaster ride. I laughed, cried and smiled. <br/><br/>After a brief, but intense, fling, Elec disappears from Greta's life for years. W</span>
  <span id="freeText14461900067210588396" style="display:none">I loved this book! I had expected the story to be kind of hard to get into after reading many reviews that said it got off to a slow start. That was not my experience at all. The story of Elec and Greta captivated me from page one. I devoured this book!<br /><br />Elec and Greta's story was full of passion, forbidden desire and angst. Reading their story took me on an emotional roller coaster ride. I laughed, cried and smiled. <br /><br />After a brief, but intense, fling, Elec disappears from Greta's life for years. When they finally cross paths again, life seems to be playing a cruel joke on them. Despite their mutual longing and intense attraction, these two just can't seem to catch a break. <br /><br />This was one of those books that kept me up late into the night. I kept telling myself I'd go to sleep when I finished the chapter, but couldn't. I had to know what was going to happen. I'm pretty sure I'll be dragging at work today but it was sooo worth it.<br /><br />I loved this story! 5 stars!<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> </span>

<div id="review_1043219570" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1043219570" />
    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1043219570?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Mysza by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14262653-mysza?shelf=favorite-read">favorite-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1043219570" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1089047118643470944"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I know I'm not supposed to care. But when it comes to you, what I'm supposed to be feeling has never seemed to matter."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420298545i/13201409._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was one angsty ride! The book was very intense and emotional. I couldn't stay away from it and kept flipping pages like crazy. I was enamoured with the story from the beginning till the end. It is divided into two parts. <br/><br/>The first one tells us how Greta and Elec met. They were step siblings, Elec came to live with Greta, her mom and his dad for a year. She want</span>
  <span id="freeText1089047118643470944" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I know I'm not supposed to care. But when it comes to you, what I'm supposed to be feeling has never seemed to matter."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420298545i/13201409._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was one angsty ride! The book was very intense and emotional. I couldn't stay away from it and kept flipping pages like crazy. I was enamoured with the story from the beginning till the end. It is divided into two parts. <br><br>The first one tells us how Greta and Elec met. They were step siblings, Elec came to live with Greta, her mom and his dad for a year. She wanted to be friends and all he did was acting like a giant dick and an asshole. But he was my kind of asshole, who in the end....wasn't really that asshole, you know. They didn't spend much time together because Elec had to go back to take care of his mother. Before he left, they somehow became friends or even more and spent one hot and sexy night together, which left their hearts broken. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You make me feel things, Greta. You always have. When I'm around you, whether it's good or bad... I feel everything. Sometimes, I don't handle it too well, and I fight it by acting like an asshole. I don't know what it is about you, but I feel like you see the real me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>After seven years, due to the family tragedy, they meet again. While Elec clearly moved on, Greta wasn't that lucky and still has feelings for him.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You were the best thing that happened to me. I hope someday I can say you were one of the best, but for now, it's only you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Once they see each other again, heart wants what it wants and makes Elec one very confused hero. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I never wanted to see you again, Greta.<br>It's so fucking good to see you again, Greta."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>While the story progresses, more facts are revealed and as Elec and Greta spend more time together, it is painfully obvious that those two are destined to be together, though nothing can be done because Elec has a new girlfriend. I know it was an issue for some of my friends, but I wasn't really put off by it, cause these things can happen in life and everything was resolved very well in the end.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>I know, the fact that he loved them both was not cool, but it's not like he didn't try. He came back for Greta later some time, found out that she was engaged and saw her happy with someone else. Since he felt not worthy of her and thought she was happy he finally let her go. He couldn't have Greta and it took him three years to eventually settle down, he met Chelsea and he fell in love again. But appearances can be deceptive, and the fact that Greta was not that happy at all and never mended her broken heart is another story.<blockquote><b><i>"I was eventually able to let Greta go only because I thought she was happy and that she was with someone who loved her. Everything I believed to get me over her was a lie. Realizing that now put my feelings back at square one even though I wouldn't be able to act on them."</i></b></blockquote>But he couldn't fully love Chelsea IMO, because his heart was always with Greta, he just wasn't aware of that while they were apart. I think this issue was well developed in the book.<br><blockquote><b><i>"I couldn't possibly fully love her if my heart beat faster for someone else. My heart hasn't shut up since it spotted you standing in that garden. I finally listened. It just took some time to clear my head enough to really understand what it wanted."<br>"There was never any contest. I loved Chelsea, but it was by default. I love you so much more. Every second I was with you again, I had to constantly reassure myself that I loved Chelsea, which is not something that you should have to do."</i></b></blockquote> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>As I said, the story is intense and emotional roller coaster, it had my heart pounding all the time. You could feel the connection between those two. It was funny, sweet and sexy in the first part. And heartbreaking and sometimes painful in the second. I was really glad for Elec's POV in the form of his book, which made some things clear. I mean, I already loved him after the first part, but his POV made me see some things different and explained everything what happened well.<br><br>I loved Elec, he is perfect material for top book boyfriend. Both the moody, hot mess teenager and all grown up Elec in glasses made my heart flutter. Greta was a good girl with an open heart and a very likeable character.<br><br>There was this one character (Greta's friend from New York) Sully, that didn't play the biggest part in the whole story, but I adored her/him, she/he had Greta's back and it was funny seeing them together.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I knew you'd be back for her, you dumb fuck."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>The ending and the epilogue was really sweet and perfect, overall the book was truly great reading, my kind of story!, and I would recommend it for all angst junkies.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/385178.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1089047118643470944" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

But when it comes to you, what I'm supposed to be feeling has never seemed to matter."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412509237i/11384485.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story follows Greta. She’s sweet, innocent good girl. When the book begins she’s only seventeen year old living with her mother and stepfather. And then one day, she gets to meet her stepbrother, Elec, who will be living in her home for their senior year. <br><br>Sweet Greta didn’t anticipate, Elec to be so… <br><br><i>Fuckin’ hot <br><br>Intense<br><br>Rough<br><br>Bad boy<br><br>And everything her wet dreams are made of.</i><br><br>But Elec is also so much more… He’s troubled, yes, but his also fragile and deep. Loveable. Amazing.<br><br>The two of them didn’t expect that their teasing and banter can lead to one amazing night and two broken hearts. <br><br>When they see each other seven years after it, it’s not in the best circumstances. Especially because of Elec’s amazing girlfriend.<br><br><b>Sexy, angsty and forbidden? Check, check and check! </b><br><br><i>Stepbrother Dearest </i> is a rollercoaster ride full of filthy talk, laugh out loud moments and sizzling sexual tension. It’s everything a fan of sexy can hope for. So, yes I really did enjoyed it! It was quick, easy read that captivated me easily. I loved the tension, the angst and Elec – the main hero, who although could be a big ass, was in reality adorable and swoon worthy. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412509605i/11384496.jpg" width="400" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Greta and Elec were absolutely cute together; I just loved them. When they were teenagers as well as adults, the chemistry between them was off the charts, and although there were some things that irked me, I didn’t let it to ruin the story for me. Even the light love triangle was bearable. <br><br>The beauty of the two of them discovering first love… Amazing. I think I swooned when the ‘rough bad boy Elec’ was showing his true self. <br><br><br><b>“I know that despite my warning, you gave me a piece of your heart anyway last night. And even though I tried to stop it, I gave you a piece of mine."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412509237i/11384488.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the explosive start to the sweet finish, <i> Stepbrother Dearest </i> was engaging read. Penelope Ward created clever, sexy little story that got my mind off problems and let me daydream for a little bit. I was turned on, I was pissed off quite few times, I also laughed so hard I probably looked like a psychiatric ward patient, because of the amazing banter between our main characters, so yes I can   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1149201173?book_show_action=true">Jan 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23285593-stepbrother-dearest">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1149201173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1062096744166758292"><b>
  <i>”“I know I’m not supposed to care. But when it comes to you, what I’m supposed to be feeling has never seemed to matter.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/> <br/>This is definitely a hit or miss type story. I totally get friend’s issues like Elec’s pov later on or that he’s kind of young to be that skilled in the bedroom and so on and so forth. For me, it was perfectly angsty and Elec was panty dropping hot and I truly fell for him while Greta was really likable and for me that’s a total win win. <br/><br/>Greta’s stepfather’s </span>
  <span id="freeText1062096744166758292" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”“I know I’m not supposed to care. But when it comes to you, what I’m supposed to be feeling has never seemed to matter.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br> <br>This is definitely a hit or miss type story. I totally get friend’s issues like Elec’s pov later on or that he’s kind of young to be that skilled in the bedroom and so on and so forth. For me, it was perfectly angsty and Elec was panty dropping hot and I truly fell for him while Greta was really likable and for me that’s a total win win. <br><br>Greta’s stepfather’s son, Elec comes to live with her during their senior year of high school. From the moment he walks in the doorway it was game on! Greta wanted him while Elec wanted to push her buttons.<br> <br><b>
  <i>"He was breathtaking…for a bastard."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492352572ra/22508269.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>This story is hot and highly entertaining and I just loved Elec. Too bad Elec’s mother needs him and he has to go back to California and so these two have one crazy hot night.<br><br><img src="https://p.gr-assets.com/540x540/fit/hostedimages/1407982905/10791656.gif%20" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>”I know that despite my warning, you gave me a piece of your heart anyway last night. And even though I tried to stop it, I gave you a piece of mine.”</i>
</b><br><br>They say their goodbyes until seven years later a death has them reuniting. Why didn’t Elec try to pursue a relationship with Greta after he left? Well, Elec felt like it would be disloyal to his mother and his mother is completely unstable as is her feelings for Greta and her mother. Do I buy it? Yes, Elec’s pov through his written story that he sends Greta was very helpful.<br> <br>Elec arrives at the funeral with his live in girlfriend, Chelsea but all the old feelings are still there for Greta. This is where things get really interesting!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492352572ra/22508267.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>”I was so confused. I never wanted to see you again, Greta. It’s so fucking good to see you again, Greta.”</i>
</b><br><br>I have to give a shout out to Sully. What a fabulous character he/she was. As for the ending, it was simply perfect.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492352572i/22508268.jpg" width="390" height="60" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>” In life, he led me to my one true love. In death, he made it possible to find her again.”</i>
</b><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1012162761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8458705688628474358">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br/><br/>4 <b> “scramble the letters” “Look at me.” </b> Kisses<br/><br/>I <b>could not</b> put this one down. And I didn’t. Seriously…I read this book, cover to cover, non-stop, in one sitting - I can’t even tell you the last time that happened…it has been a while but <b>OMG</b> I effin loved it! Everything about it completely had me…I was just compelled to keep reading, I couldn’t even fathom <i>not</i> finishing it because every time I said I was going to stop…something else happened and I was like…wel</span>
  <span id="freeText8458705688628474358" style="display:none">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br><br>4 <b> “scramble the letters” “Look at me.” </b> Kisses<br><br>I <b>could not</b> put this one down. And I didn’t. Seriously…I read this book, cover to cover, non-stop, in one sitting - I can’t even tell you the last time that happened…it has been a while but <b>OMG</b> I effin loved it! Everything about it completely had me…I was just compelled to keep reading, I couldn’t even fathom <i>not</i> finishing it because every time I said I was going to stop…something else happened and I was like…well, I can’t stop <i>now</i>!!! And so…I sit here writing my review on barely four hours of sleep and I seriously cannot stop thinking about Greta and her ass hole step brother and the rollercoaster ride they just took me on. *<i>sigh</i>* #BookwormProblems<br><br>Greta Hansen…is a sweetheart. A little on the innocent side…friendly…kind…but to her very core a sweet girl. I mean only a sweet person would be nice to someone who is as much of an ass as Elec is to her. But don’t let any of that fool you, Greta is not a doormat by any stretch of the imagination…she just picks her battles wisely and stands up for what she believes in. I bonded with Greta in ways I wasn’t expecting…she’s an only child, and so am I…she lost her father very quickly to cancer and so did I. I think that’s why I really fell into the story, I may not have connected 100% to Greta, but I <i>got</i> her and I liked her <b>a lot</b>. I think anyone who has the balls to stand up to a guy like Elec deserves a gold medal, honestly…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412041400i/11315288._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> ‘I left the room and went back downstairs. Seeing him looking so down when he didn’t know I was watching him made me more determined than ever to break through to him somehow. I needed to know if this was just a façade or if he were truly a genuine asshole. The meaner he was to me, the more I wanted to make him like me. It was a challenge.’ </b> </blockquote><br>Elec O’Rourke…yeah…even his name is hot…but trust me…he only gets hotter…tall, lean muscles, tattoo’s everywhere (and the fact that they actually meant something! Don’t even get me started…), dark hair, grey eyes…but it was his attitude that <i>really</i> sucked me in. He’s an ass…cocky…arrogant…but not in a douchey way…he toed that line very nicely. While he may have said and done things to Greta to get a reaction from her, I honestly didn’t think any of his actions were truly mean or mean-spirited. There is <i>so</i> much more to Elec than meets the eye…I mean, I get people who have it rough growing up…rough would have been a cake walk compared to what Elec went through and just thinking about his childhood makes me tear up Needless to say, he is a momma’s boy, through and through, but I don’t think she could have dreamed up a better son than Elec. I loved that beneath the tough, tatt’d guy was a sweet, gentle heart…I loved that he was a writer…and I loved that he really only opened up to one person…the one girl he wasn’t supposed to love.<br><br><blockquote> <b> “Don’t do that.”<br>“What?”<br>“You turned away from me. That’s my fault. I made you feel like I didn’t want you looking at me – that self-respect bullshit I fed you. Out of everything I ever said to you, that was the <i>biggest</i> lie, and I regret it the most. I’d started to let my guard down, and it freaked me out. I never had a problem with the way you look at me. My issue is the way it makes <i>me</i> feel when you look at me; things I’m not supposed to feel, things I <i>can’t</i> let myself feel for you. At the same time…nothing felt worse than when you <i>stopped</i> looking at me Greta.” </b> </blockquote><br>Oye…where do I start with these two. Why is that I enjoy it to no end when a couple is at odds with one another? I <b>love it</b> when they fight…maybe it’s because it’s a passionate emotion of some kind and I know buried behind that anger or frustration or whatever…is the truth. Elec is an ass to Greta from the start…he barely even looks at her and he’s giving her an attitude so I <i>knew</i> it had very little to do with Greta and a whole lot to do with something or someone else. I loved Greta’s faith and devotion to Elec…he gives her every reason to hate him…give up on him…and she doesn’t. The way they form their bond…over ice cream and video games…protecting one another from the things they can…it was like I didn’t even have to try to fall in love with them…it just happened…but man did they make it a rough ride. And I thoroughly enjoyed every second of it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412041400ra/11315289.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> “You make me feel things, Greta. You always have. When I’m around you, whether it’s good or bad…I feel everything. Sometimes, I don’t handle it too well, and I fight it by acting like an asshole. I don’t know what it is about you, but I feel like you see the real me. The second I saw you again for the first time at Greg’s when you were standing in that garden…it was like I couldn’t hide behind myself anymore.” </b> </blockquote><br>I’m an angst whore and <i>Stepbrother Dearest</i> fed my angsty soul! So the book is separated into two parts. Part 1…<b>OMG</b>…the sexual tension was palpable and delicious and I was tortured…and then, things got…hotter than hell. Good gravy…Elec is a sexual force of nature and he may or may not have made me drool (he totally made me drool). Clearly…I’m in my happy little bookworm place with Part 1 and I knew it was about to get angsty again but…I was <b>not</b> prepared for the angst that came next. If I was tortured in Part 1…Part 2 nearly ripped my heart out. Because…it’s still the same angsty goodness with these characters…just more history, with a side of pent up emotions and a dollop of I-still-wanna-fuck-your-brains-out…sounds like a tasty recipe, right? Oh…it <b>totally</b> was. Obviously, the writing was what brought this all together for me and made it that much better. It was fantastic…clearly…I mean, for me it was un-put-downable (yes…it’s a word!)…I mean the story just demanded to be read. It was angsty, hot-n-steamy, funny, emotional and it flowed perfectly. I’ll be honest…this was my first <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7105545.Penelope_Ward" title="Penelope Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Penelope Ward</a>, but if this is what I can expect from her…count me in cause I’m in love. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412041400ra/11315290.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote> <b> “I guess it doesn’t matter anymore,” I said under my breath so low that I didn’t think he heard me.<br>Elec scowled as he took the empty bowl to the sink, washed it and put it in the strainer.<br>He looked back at me. “You’ll always matter to me, Greta. Always.” </b> </blockquote><br>So clearly…I enjoyed the story, loved the characters, everything was great...but there was part towards the end of the book that I got a little frustrated with. The entire book is from Greta’s POV…but there is a point where we get to see things from Elec’s POV…and I don’t want to say why or how because I feel that would spoil it…but trust me, I was <b>so</b> excited when it happened because the entire book all I wanted to do was climb into that boy’s head! So I’m loving every minute of it until…it got repetitive. I am a lover of dual POV’s, so do not get me wrong on this but I like it up until the point where I stop getting new information. There were certain pieces that I felt did not need to be rehashed word for word…I wasn’t reading anything I hadn’t already read before, and that’s where my frustration came into play. Plus…with what was happening, I almost wanted more from Greta…of her thoughts and emotions from what she is learning. Then towards the end, it all wrapped up so quickly…I felt like I didn’t get to enjoy it as much as I would have liked. Don’t get me wrong, the ending is fabulous…I guess maybe a little more conversation and it would have made me feel better about everything.<br><br><blockquote> <b> “Now, I understand,” Sully said.<br>“Understand what?”<br>“Why you’re here with me every Friday night and not on a date with some man, why you’ve been unable to open your heart to anyone. It belongs to someone else.”<br>“It used to. Now, it’s just broken. How do I fix it?”<br>“Sometimes, we can’t.” </b> </blockquote><br>I was not expecting the ending to be as…thorough as it was. Of course I was hopeful for my big red bow that I love to get…but this was more than I could have ever imagined and the epilogue just thrilled me to bits and pieces. And the fact that it was from Elec’s POV was pretty spectacular. I’m always the girl who wants more, but this is an absolutely fantastic standalone. <i>Stepbrother Dearest</i> is packed full of so much amazingness...an amazing story of two people, the choices they made and the unending love they had for each other.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412041400i/11315291._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874066.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434116i/874067.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8458705688628474358" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1020736378" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1020736378" />
    <a title="Mariℓina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12824955-mari-ina"><img alt="Mariℓina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575879635p2/12824955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1020736378?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mariℓina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mariℓina" href="/user/show/12824955-mari-ina">Mariℓina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12824955-mari-ina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1020736378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12334213148859847570">4,5 Stars, I loved it! <br/>Although <b>Stepbrother Dearest</b> had a sad vibe I couldn't explain in the beginning, now that I've read the whole story I can say with all of my heart, that it is amazing. Filled with many funny moments, interesting characters and a much deeper "meaning" than I thought it would have. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412256146i/11346226._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Get Cereal = Elec and Greta.<br/>Elec was a compelling character. For a bad-boy he was quite responsible and wholesome and also after all his secrets are finally out, his actions are much more understa</span>
  <span id="freeText12334213148859847570" style="display:none">4,5 Stars, I loved it! <br>Although <b>Stepbrother Dearest</b> had a sad vibe I couldn't explain in the beginning, now that I've read the whole story I can say with all of my heart, that it is amazing. Filled with many funny moments, interesting characters and a much deeper "meaning" than I thought it would have. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412256146i/11346226._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Get Cereal = Elec and Greta.<br>Elec was a compelling character. For a bad-boy he was quite responsible and wholesome and also after all his secrets are finally out, his actions are much more understandable and even reasonable. He was a little tormentor, with a funny side but I appreciate the fact that he was always very protective of Greta.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412256146i/11346227._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Greta was an all-around sweet girl, she gave her heart once and that was it for her. For seven years she tries her best to achieve in living a life without Elec, without much success that's for sure. So the very moment he is back, she can't help it. She can't forget. She won't stop. They were meant for each other and the chemistry is still very much alive.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1407347682ra/10678992.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book is divided into two parts. The first takes place in their teenage years and the second after 7 years when they finally meet again. The first part ends with a heartbreaking goodbye and the second part is dominated by their strong feelings and Elec's side of events told in a refreshing way.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412256146i/11346228._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked the writing style a lot, and I found Elec's way of telling his story genius, although a little bit repetitive in the dialogue it was very entertaining and so revealing. His story of how he went to New York in order to find her had me in tears.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382846198ra/6234769.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All in all, there is a hot, tattooed and pierced *wink, wink* bad boy who knows how to play with words and hearts. He transforms himself and becomes a helper, a role-model even, for those in need. And an incredible heroine, fueled by determination, with a kind open heart -she could have been a bitch to Chelsea, but she wasn't- and so much love to give. But of course let's not forget the brilliant, heartwarming storyline which was excellent. Yes, this is one of the best step-brother romances you can find.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412257906ra/11346469.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>THOUGHTS ABOUT THE BOOK<br><br>- Their first time was very intimate and life altering for both of them.<br>- The anagrams were an interesting touch. <br>- I didn't like Victoria. <br>- His life was weird and crazy from the beginning.<br>- Sally was awesome. <br>- Chelsea was a good girl, I mostly hate the "other" woman in books, but she was lovable.<br>- The ending was beautiful.</span>
