<div id="review_1184566257" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1184566257" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1184566257?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23285593-stepbrother-dearest">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Brandi by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=angst">angst</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1184566257" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16098581601801246584"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422891716i/13559620._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Stepbrother Dearest</i> was a fast-paced, angsty ride. When Greata's new stepbrother moves in, he is not want she expected. Elec and his father have a difficult relationship. The last thing he wants to do is move in with him and his new family, but with his mother going out to the country for a year and he is out of options. Elec is rude, confrontational, and Greta is extremely attracted to him.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>"Physically, he was my dream and in every other way, my nightmare."</b>
</i> <br/><br/>These two get off to a rough start</span>
  <span id="freeText16098581601801246584" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422891716i/13559620._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Stepbrother Dearest</i> was a fast-paced, angsty ride. When Greata's new stepbrother moves in, he is not want she expected. Elec and his father have a difficult relationship. The last thing he wants to do is move in with him and his new family, but with his mother going out to the country for a year and he is out of options. Elec is rude, confrontational, and Greta is extremely attracted to him.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Physically, he was my dream and in every other way, my nightmare."</b>
</i> <br><br>These two get off to a rough start, but as time passes, Greta discovers there is more to Elec than meets the eye. They grow closer and try desperately to fight their attraction to on another.<br><br><b>
  <i>"You're the only girl in the entire world that's forbidden, and fuck me if that doesn't make me want you more than anything."</i>
</b> <br><br>Just as things are starting to progress, Elec gets a phone call that changes everything. With goodbye fast approaching, these two share one special night.<br><br><i>
  <b>"I want to be the only one to show you everything and to be the one you'll always remember for the rest of your life."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422890784ra/13559391.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Years pass, now, 7 years later, a family tragedy brings Elec back into Greta's life. A lot has changed, or has it? <br><br><i>
  <b>"You were the best thing that ever happen to me. I hope that someday I can say you were one of the best, but for now, it's only you."</b>
</i><br><br>I enjoyed this one, it was full of angst and sexual tension. Greta and Elec were likeable, and I was pulling for them throughout this story. I do feel like some of the Elec's POV during the second half could have been condensed, but overall it was an enjoyable read for me. I love my jerky guys ;) </span>
  <a data-text-id="16098581601801246584" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1062611363" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062611363" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062611363?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062611363" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11509675629208361677"><br/>Was it the title, the hype, or me? <br/><br/>This one was just okay to me. I went into thinking I would love this one. I mean I love forbidden love, sneaking around, hot taboo sex, but that isn't what we get here. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412477257i/11381260._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>The story starts with Elec coming to live with his father and his new family. Greta is excited to meet Elec, and Elec is a complete dick to her. He is miserable in Boston, hates his father and decides being an ass to Greta will make things better for him. <br/><br/>So here we are at the beginning, we have</span>
  <span id="freeText11509675629208361677" style="display:none"><br>Was it the title, the hype, or me? <br><br>This one was just okay to me. I went into thinking I would love this one. I mean I love forbidden love, sneaking around, hot taboo sex, but that isn't what we get here. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412477257i/11381260._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The story starts with Elec coming to live with his father and his new family. Greta is excited to meet Elec, and Elec is a complete dick to her. He is miserable in Boston, hates his father and decides being an ass to Greta will make things better for him. <br><br>So here we are at the beginning, we have the asshole stepbrother and the sweet and innocent stepsister, this was my least favorite part of the book. All of their interactions were very juvenile and really wore on me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412476458ra/11381163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>We have a lot of back and forth: Elec is an ass, Greta makes excuses for him and decides to kill him with kindness, Elec feels bad and is nice to Greta for a little while - rinse and repeat. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394052554ra/8801617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>After one epic night together Elec leaves. They never plan to see each other again, but after seven years they are brought back together.<br><br>I won't go any further as I don't want to spoil the plot of anyone. <br><br><b>My thoughts</b><br><br>Cocky assholes are usually my thing and I did enjoy Elec, but throw in the immaturity it was just too much. We do end up getting both POV's in the story. I liked knowing Elec's POV, but the way this one is done it was basically retelling the same story I had just read. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386381496ra/7351566.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I wish I could say I loved this one, I went into it thinking I would. I actually couldn't wait to start it today, but in the end it was just okay. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403212ra/784354.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Lastly, I can't end this review without saying - If I never see another anagram it will be too soon. </span>

<div id="review_1057796609" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1057796609" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1057796609?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=panty-soaking-read">panty-soaking-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=angsty-read">angsty-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1057796609" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8596831958453166488"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br/><i>{BR with Mel, Dee, and Sharon}</i><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/f05efcee27effdbc654cb2e969685fb5_zpsa8770c6e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412530973i/11387238._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo f05efcee27effdbc654cb2e969685fb5_zpsa8770c6e.jpg' width='340' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>This is the first Penelope Ward book I've read and I wasn't sure what to expect from all of the conflicting reviews on GR. I went in completely blind. I looked at reviews but skimmed only for fear of coming across any spoilers.<br/>I was sucked into the story from the very beginning!!! I was so pleasantly surprised at how much I enjoyed this one. It was funny, heart breaking, angsty, and had some pretty amazing sexy times as well!! PLUS a HOT new </span>
  <span id="freeText8596831958453166488" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br><i>{BR with Mel, Dee, and Sharon}</i><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/f05efcee27effdbc654cb2e969685fb5_zpsa8770c6e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412530973i/11387238._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo f05efcee27effdbc654cb2e969685fb5_zpsa8770c6e.jpg" width="340" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This is the first Penelope Ward book I've read and I wasn't sure what to expect from all of the conflicting reviews on GR. I went in completely blind. I looked at reviews but skimmed only for fear of coming across any spoilers.<br>I was sucked into the story from the very beginning!!! I was so pleasantly surprised at how much I enjoyed this one. It was funny, heart breaking, angsty, and had some pretty amazing sexy times as well!! PLUS a HOT new book boyfriend with a pierced penis!! HOLY HELL!!!<br><br><br><br>Greta Hansen is a HS senior who is your typical good girl. She doesn't ever get into trouble and loves to read. She lives with her mother and step father in Boston. Her life is about to be turned upside down, when she meets her step brother, Elec, for the first time. He's coming to live with them for a year while his mother works in London on a teaching assignment. These two get off on the wrong foot almost immediately due to Elec's rude and antagonistic behavior. He's got a chip on his shoulder and obviously there is a huge amount of tension between him and his Dad.<br><br><br><br>I will say at the 2% mark, my jaw hit the floor, and I was wishing I was Greta when she walked in on Elec getting out of the shower. I think I'd have stood there ogling him in all his glory as well. As soon as she's describing his huge pierced penis, I was drooling and started to fall a little in love with him.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/full_zps8a48cdcd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412530973ra/11387239.gif" alt=" photo full_zps8a48cdcd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Greta tries hard to get through Elec's impenetrable wall, and as time passes the two can't help but start to fall for each other. I loved that Elec was a writer and that he opened up to Greta by letting her read one of his stories. <br>Their feelings are starting to grow much deeper for each other and then they're suddenly torn apart when Elec's mom ends up coming home early and so he must return back to California.<br><br><br>That last night they shared was pretty damn HOT. I did keep asking myself..<b>"how are these two going at it when their parents are in the room down the hall????"</b> Oh well, it worked for me anyway, so I wasn't going to harp on that too much.<br><br><br>Elec leaves the next day, and it will be <b>SEVEN YEARS</b> before they see each other again!!! He did text her once, a year after he had left.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>I still dream about your neck. I still think about you every day. For some reason, I just needed you to know that tonight. Please don't write back.</b>
</i><br><br><br>Seven years later, tragedy strikes which causes the two to reunite, but it was so heartbreaking because Elec shows up with a girlfriend. Greta had been engaged a while back but had broken things off. She never got over Elec and every man she ever had been with just didn't measure up to him. It was clear that when they were in the same room, the feelings between them were just as strong as they were all those years ago.<br><br><br><b>"You make me feel things, Greta. You always have. When I'm around you, whether it's good or bad...I feel</b> <i>
  <b>everything</b>
</i>.<br><br><br><br>They end up spending some time alone together and each struggle with how they are feeling and Elec is battling with his sense of loyalty to his girlfriend. Again there's a moment where I started to get a little teary eyed. Angst ensues here and I didn't know how much more I could take. I desperately wanted an HEA for these two.<br><br><br><br>I really fell in love with these two and their story. I could go on and on, but who wants to read a long review anyway?? I am glad that I went in blind and am definitely planning on reading other books by this author. Sometimes there are books that the majority seems to hate but you love, and vice versa. We all have our own opinions and tastes, and I love chatting with people who had a different experience with a book than I did. This one just grabbed me on all levels and my buddy reading partners all agreed. :)<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8596831958453166488" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1012194063" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13664492195201203117"> <b> 4,5 STARS<br/><br/>"I've been ready since the day I walked in the door,took one look at you and realized I was fucked." </b><br/><br/>This was an absolutely fantastic read. I loved the way this story developed, progressing the characters love story from teenagers and then seven years later as adults. I fell more and more in love with this couple with each and every page. Their story is sweet, funny, hot and very intense.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423830566ra/13679164.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/> When we first meet Greta and Elec, they are 17 years old and are forced to live together because </span>
  <span id="freeText13664492195201203117" style="display:none"> <b> 4,5 STARS<br><br>"I've been ready since the day I walked in the door,took one look at you and realized I was fucked." </b><br><br>This was an absolutely fantastic read. I loved the way this story developed, progressing the characters love story from teenagers and then seven years later as adults. I fell more and more in love with this couple with each and every page. Their story is sweet, funny, hot and very intense.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423830566ra/13679164.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br> When we first meet Greta and Elec, they are 17 years old and are forced to live together because Elec's father married Greta's mother. Elec comes to live with them for a period of time. He wasn't very lovable in the beginning, he was rude, cocky and mean to Greta. Elec tries to resist his feelings for Greta, but as they begin to spend more time together, he finds himself unable to deny their attraction. Just as Elec finally makes his move, something happens that forces Elec to leave sooner than planned, and they both say goodbye forever. Seven years later, tragedy strikes and these two meet again. Are their feelings for one another still strong? How will things end for these two?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423830566i/13679163._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I absolutely loved these two characters. They felt so real to me and Greta just so loveable! She has strong feelings for Elec and she knew that underneath his cockiness there was a sweet guy. Elec intrigued me from the first moment I meet him and I just knew that there was more in him. He is smart, hot, funny and so protective over Greta. He made a great book boyfriend! Ms. Ward definitely knows how to write hot sex scenes! They was hot, passionate and intense!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424100663i/13715819._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br>This book is written in two parts. The first part was good as they are teens but the second was even better as adults. I experienced so many feelings while I was reading it. The story was told from Greta's POV but we get a glimpse into Elec's head and his POV. The epilogue was one of the best parts of the book and it made me love Elec even more!! I haven't read a taboo book before so I was worried that these two coming together would make me feel uncomfortable but the fact is I loved the story and all their hurdles and wasn’t uncomfortable at all.<br><br><b> "I fucking love you too.I don't think I realized how much until I saw you again."</b><br> <br>This story had everything I would want in a book and much more. I highly recommend friends meeting Elec and Greta!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1554835758" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3487283054572582978">Elec and Greta take us on an emotional roller coaster that begins when they meet as teens and share a reluctant but very present connection. A connection that is technically forbidden as they are step siblings. The tension between them is palatable, mounting, and full of sensual moments. One night, it comes to a head and the next day, Elec has to leave to take care of something important. Time passes and Elec is brought back into her life at an emotional moment. Where there once was fire, there </span>
  <span id="freeText3487283054572582978" style="display:none">Elec and Greta take us on an emotional roller coaster that begins when they meet as teens and share a reluctant but very present connection. A connection that is technically forbidden as they are step siblings. The tension between them is palatable, mounting, and full of sensual moments. One night, it comes to a head and the next day, Elec has to leave to take care of something important. Time passes and Elec is brought back into her life at an emotional moment. Where there once was fire, there are sparks but Elec didn't come back alone. He brought someone. It's interesting to read our H and h navigate through a very intense emotional minefield. He doesn't physically cheat. There's no doubt of that, but there's an emotional component that can put people on edge. He goes back to figure things out all the while the word love gets thrown out in a way that made me cringe a bit. One of the biggest areas of opportunity for me in this book was in not revealing what happened when he went back. I felt like there was a hole there. Then there was Elec's mother. That situation was sort of glossed over as well. In the end I had quite a few questions so it didn't wrap up as well as I would've liked but all in all, it was a good read and quite hottt. ( Ahem ) I especially like the piercing **cough**sexyashell**cough**.</span>

<div id="review_1018459501" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1018459501" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1018459501?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1018459501" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14931571550082661407"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You were the best thing that ever happened to me. I hope someday I can say you were one of the best, but for now, it’s only you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>You know those books that pull you in like a riptide, taking over all your senses and making you completely oblivious to the fact that there is a real life outside those pages waiting for you to live it? Well, this is one of <i>those</i> books. From the moment I read the title, something inside me started screaming, <i>I want</i>, the mere idea of a forbidden romance of</span>
  <span id="freeText14931571550082661407" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You were the best thing that ever happened to me. I hope someday I can say you were one of the best, but for now, it’s only you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>You know those books that pull you in like a riptide, taking over all your senses and making you completely oblivious to the fact that there is a real life outside those pages waiting for you to live it? Well, this is one of <i>those</i> books. From the moment I read the title, something inside me started screaming, <i>I want</i>, the mere idea of a forbidden romance of this type making my skin tingle. However, nothing about this story is what I expected to find, and everything about it has been a wonderful surprise—from the confident prose, to the dynamic characters, this is a love story that I immersed myself into fully and wholeheartedly, and loved every single minute of it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Physically, he was my dream and in every other way, my nightmare.”</i>
</blockquote><br>We meet Greta and Elec as teenagers on the very day they first meet, when Elec comes to live temporarily with his estranged dad and his new family. Even though they have technically been stepsiblings for a few years at that stage, they are complete strangers to one another, and while we see Greta looking forward to getting to know her new stepbrother, from the first moment Elec enters his new home, he does so with an air of disapproval and rebellion. And his main target seems to be the very person who is most enthusiastic about his arrival—Greta. The more young Greta tries to make him feel welcome in his new home, the more scorn and rejection she suffers at the hands of her new stepbrother. And yet, she never gives up, her innate kind-heartedness successfully bringing down Elec’s defensive walls, one brick at a time.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The meaner he was to me, the more I wanted to make him like me.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Elec is a contradiction at first. Smug, defiant, even apathetic at times, he is the kind of teenager you want to dislike. And yet his every cantankerous and hurtful action indicates a deeper, more serious cause at the root of it all. We see snippets of his problematic relationship with his father, leaving us suspecting that everything about Elec’s negative attitude is a protective shield, and nothing about him is as he wishes the world around him to think. He is complicated, difficult to warm up to, but his faults make him a truly three-dimensional character in our eyes.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“… nothing felt worse than when you stopped looking at me, Greta.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Greta is his antithesis—innocent and somewhat naïve, she is the kind of girl who feels freely, openly, unreservedly because that is the way she has been loved all her life, and she is also the kind of heroine we cannot help but love from the start. As much as she fights it, her body’s reaction to Elec and his bad-boy appearance is something she is unable to hide, leaving her open to his mockery and fickle behaviour. He irks her, winds her up, embarrasses her, but she remains incapable of controlling his effect on her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Holy hell… his tip was pierced. What a way to be introduced to my first live one.”</i>
</blockquote><br>As Greta’s quiet persistence eventually pays off and they start building a shaky friendship, her growing protectiveness and unwavering kindness towards him become the foundations of his first true human connection. But the closer they get, the harder it becomes to fight their mutual attraction, and they keep slipping, failing at every turn, their bodies desperately craving one another, while their hearts ache to connect on a deeper level. One night in each other’s arms, however, is all they get, one night of uninhibited passion, indulging their every secret fantasy and heart’s desire, and then it all suddenly ends. They part ways. And they don’t see each other again for seven long years during which Greta’s heartbreak never subsides.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I’d rather have one night with you than nothing at all.”</i>
</blockquote><br>When life finally forces their paths to cross again, they are no longer the same people they once were. Greta has grown into a confident, strong young woman whose heart might have never recovered from losing the only man she has ever truly loved, but she has moved on from her heartbreak, adjusted, learned to live with it. Seeing Elec after all those years, and given the tragic circumstances of their unexpected meeting, brings a lot of her childhood insecurities to the surface, one look at him alone reminding her of what they once shared and everything she has desperately tried to forget over the years. But she remains strong, bottling up her feelings the best she can.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“He was hers. I was his. It. Was. F*cked. Up.”</i>
</blockquote><br>And this is where this story turns from heartbreakingly angsty to outright agonising. Greta’s silent pain from seeing that Elec has moved on with his life and perhaps never shared the same feelings as hers is as acute as it is compelling. Hearing her every thought, seeing her every vulnerability being tested, watching her heart break before our eyes all over again is something that made every protective bone in my body come to life. I was enraged, inconsolable, almost hysterical in my reactions to Greta’s inner turmoil, her every emotion becoming my own.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The “one that got away” was supposed to stay away, not come back and leave you all over again.”</i>
</blockquote><br>But, as it happens so often in life, there is another side to every story. And this story is no exception. Ms Ward stuns us into silence with a unique twist, a rare chance to hear what we were only left speculating about, and what we get to discover went beyond my wildest dreams. I adored that aspect of the story, even when I felt it was given in too much detail and could have been offered to the reader in broader strokes with fewer repetitions. It added so much colour to the story, so many extra layers for us to ponder upon, making Greta and Elec two well-rounded, almost real characters popping out from these pages. This is a story that made me <i>feel</i> beginning to end—from heartbroken to hot and bothered, from angry to utterly elated—and it was one of those reading experiences that only got better the more time I spent analysing the characters. I most certainly did not expect to find this many layers in a story of this type, but every last one of them has left me gobsmacked. This was an addictive ‘angst-fest’ cover to cover, sexy and emotional all at the same time, and one I highly recommend.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“We just have tonight. Please…don’t hold back.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>[4.5 STARS]</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382869i/740934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2014/09/29/stepbrother-dearest-penelope-ward/" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a> | <a href="http://www.twitter.com/natashabkjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Twitter!</a><br><br>Amazon US: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1ywkzYz">http://amzn.to/1ywkzYz</a><br>Amazon UK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1BtXEtg">http://amzn.to/1BtXEtg</a><br>Amazon CA: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1uwu1Zp">http://amzn.to/1uwu1Zp</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14931571550082661407" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I was not a fan of Elec. I thought he was an cocky ass (and not the good kind) and didn't really see what Greta saw in him, other than a hot body. I just couldn't connect with him at all. <div id="review_1410773606" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1410773606" />
    <a title="⊱ Poppy ⊰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47555322-poppy"><img alt="⊱ Poppy ⊰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475924055p2/47555322.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1410773606?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="⊱ Poppy ⊰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="⊱ Poppy ⊰" href="/user/show/47555322-poppy">⊱ Poppy ⊰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47555322-poppy?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47555322-poppy?shelf=2016">2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1410773606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2198848192127828450"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471698617ra/20094153.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You were the best thing that ever happen to me. I hope that someday I can say you were one of the best, but for now, it's only you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Well, I'll be honest if it wouldn't have been for my friends here, i wouldn't even have picked this book. Although the <b>Title</b> really attract me, but after so many fail reads of stepbrother & sister love, i was really wary to pick this one out. But after reading so many 5star reviews, i just decided to pick this out. And i am glad i picked it out. This wa</span>
  <span id="freeText2198848192127828450" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471698617ra/20094153.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You were the best thing that ever happen to me. I hope that someday I can say you were one of the best, but for now, it's only you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Well, I'll be honest if it wouldn't have been for my friends here, i wouldn't even have picked this book. Although the <b>Title</b> really attract me, but after so many fail reads of stepbrother &amp; sister love, i was really wary to pick this one out. But after reading so many 5star reviews, i just decided to pick this out. And i am glad i picked it out. This was some fresh read for me and i loved it.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22843341.Stepbrother_Dearest" title="Stepbrother Dearest by Penelope Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Stepbrother Dearest</a> was not our usual stepbrother and sister forbidden love. It was quite a unique read for me. At many turn i found myself gaping at how the plot changed in front of me. The usual drama/taboo that consist forbidden love was not there. and i am glad it wasn't. It really bug me out. The Drama is one of my pet peeve. Though this book really lack any kind of drama. And because of that i am really thankful of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7105545.Penelope_Ward" title="Penelope Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Penelope Ward</a>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471697402ra/20093811.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I never had a problem with the way you look at me. My issue is the way it makes me feel when you look at me: things I’m not supposed to feel, things I <b>can’t</b> let myself feel for you. At the same time …nothing felt worse than when you <b>stopped</b> looking at me, Greta.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Elec</b> has become of of my bookish boyfriend. He has everything that i want in a book-boyfriend. <i>His cockiness, his attitude, his tattoo's, his inner writer, &amp; blah blah blah.</i> Elec really was an exception of the forbidden love between a stepbrother and sister. At starring we got to know the <i>asshole and dick Elec</i>, but as story take place we got know the Elec who was truly a loving person, and the one who was getting mentally abused by his own father. A Elec who dearly loved his mom with his every being. And a Elec who was so protective and possessive if it came to Greta, not in a brotherly love but as an attraction and <i>Possibly love!!</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471697402i/20093812._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471697402ra/20093813.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471697402ra/20093814.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I want to be the only one to show you everything and to be the one you'll always remember for the rest of your life.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Greta &amp; Elec</b>, they together just blown my mind away. I loved how they both were trying so hard to stay away. The chemistry was <i>so intense and ohhh myy hot, sooo hot.</i> But things can't go the way you wanted to and it happened with Elec &amp; Greta too. As soon as they were together, there time chase to over as soon as it started. <br><br>Elec had to go back to his mother and there was so going back. they had to fall apart. But tragedy happens and his father Randy had a heart-attack and died and that led Elec and Greta back to the square one from where they started. But nothing were same, Elec had an girlfriend whom he supposed he love. But the feeling he had for Greta came back crashing him to oblivion with the loss of his father, he didn't take things well. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He was hers. <br>I was his. <br>It. Was. Fucked. Up.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>To avoid getting in funeral and from a panic attack; Greta made Elec ignore the funeral and got to drive him for one last night, before he have to go back to Chelsea and they again have to say goodbye. But can they ignore the feelings they had for each other for so many years, with Greta having no one at her side. With Chelsea on picture would Elec acknowledged his feelings that had never died for Greta or again faith will take them apart.??<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The "one that got away" was supposed to stay away, not come back and leave you all over again.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471697402ra/20093815.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471697402ra/20093816.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471697402ra/20093817.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I loved every single thing of this book with the fucking <b>amazing</b> plot twist and a story to break and cheer up your heart. Give it a go!!</i><br><b>Totally Recommended!!</b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1067068301" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer467199222595989373"><b>3 STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406804520i/10599887._SX540_.jpg' alt='' height='300' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Genre:</b> NA romance<br/><b>Cover:</b> 8/10<br/><b>Writing:</b> 8/10<br/><b>Heroine:</b> 4/10<br/><b>Hero:</b> 7/10<br/><b>Humour:</b> 2/10<br/><b>Hotness:</b> 7/10<br/><b>Romance:</b> 6/10<br/><b>Extra book Details:</b> Heroine POV; 1st person. Stand-alone. Approx 290 kindle pages.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>When Greta sees her new Stepbrother for the first time, she can't help but be overwhelmed with lust.... That is, until he opens his mouth.<br/><br/>Living with him in such close quarters proves quite the challenge, Elec is a man-whoring, smoking (in more ways that one), tatted asshole that just loves to get under h</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText467199222595989373" style="display:none"><b>3 STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406804520i/10599887._SX540_.jpg" alt="" height="300" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Genre:</b> NA romance<br><b>Cover:</b> 8/10<br><b>Writing:</b> 8/10<br><b>Heroine:</b> 4/10<br><b>Hero:</b> 7/10<br><b>Humour:</b> 2/10<br><b>Hotness:</b> 7/10<br><b>Romance:</b> 6/10<br><b>Extra book Details:</b> Heroine POV; 1st person. Stand-alone. Approx 290 kindle pages.<br><br><b>
  <i>When Greta sees her new Stepbrother for the first time, she can't help but be overwhelmed with lust.... That is, until he opens his mouth.<br><br>Living with him in such close quarters proves quite the challenge, Elec is a man-whoring, smoking (in more ways that one), tatted asshole that just loves to get under her skin. But she still wishes he'd get in her pants.<br><br>Unfortunately Elec is definitely more than what's on the surface, and soon Greta starts to fall for her broken, talented, foul-mouthed Stepbrother.</i>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He was my dream and in every other way, my nightmare.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407594236i/10744003.jpg" alt="" height="20" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>'Stepbrother Dearest' is a really hard book for me to rate. <b>I'm so conflicted (much like Elec was towards Greta)...</b><br><br>It was one of those books where <b>I wished I could have changed it around and made it a better read for me.</b><br>I really loved the beginning. <b>I loved the push and pull, the banter, the insults, the innuendoes... Elec's filthy and insulting mouth.</b><br><br>Most of the time Elec was one of those asshole heroes that says and does something awesome, or shows you the most vulnerable part of him. Making you fall for him harder. <br><br>But it didn't last long. I found myself peeved at the <b>jealousy overload</b>, which increased in volume throughout the book and found myself in the middle of a <b>FMF love-triangle</b>. There was one part that really pushed my hard-limits; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the part where after lusting over Greta, Elec pounces on his girlfriend and thinks of Greta, thought not descriptive, I had to hear that he did this - four times. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The fact that Elec likes her because she's 'pretty/hot' and 'understands the real him' wasn't enough for me.<br><br><b>I wished he'd fallen for her as a person... There were also times when I felt that Greta needed some self-respect</b>.<br><br>At 66% there was a whole 20% of the book dedicated to Elec's POV. It was a<b> repetition of all the major scenes in the book.</b> It was very much unneeded, you only had to read between the lines to know what was going on in Elec's head.<br><br><b>I started liking again towards the last 20%.</b> The sex was hot... Elec could say the most wonderful things and I really liked the conclusion.<br><br><b>My 3 stars this time isn't for 'an average read', it's for a read that was equal parts - really good and turn-offable.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407252752i/10663054.jpg" alt="" height="110" width="210" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1012225502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6093295575397266993"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421464i/837220._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 3.75 FORBIDDEN STARS♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413769136i/11560482._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"You're the only girl in the entire world that's forbidden, and fuck me if that doesn't make me want you more than anything."<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>I'm not quite sure what I was expecting to get when I started this book. I for sure liked it for the most part, but I can't say that I loved it like so many others did. Still, it was really good.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412651085i/11402471._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Since the moment I read the blurb and saw tha</span>
  <span id="freeText6093295575397266993" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421464i/837220._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 3.75 FORBIDDEN STARS♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413769136i/11560482._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You're the only girl in the entire world that's forbidden, and fuck me if that doesn't make me want you more than anything."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I'm not quite sure what I was expecting to get when I started this book. I for sure liked it for the most part, but I can't say that I loved it like so many others did. Still, it was really good.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412651085i/11402471._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Since the moment I read the blurb and saw that awesome cover, I knew I had to read this. The book is told in Greta's POV, though, we do get Elec's POV later on. There are also two parts in this book. I was not expecting the second part in this book. When I started reading, I assumed this would continue with Elec and Greta being seventeen year old teens. But in part two, you get to see them as adults. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I want to be the first one to show you everything and to be the one you'll always remember for the rest of your life."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Greta has been an only child her whole life, that changes when her Step Father Randy decides to bring his son Elec to come live with them. Greta can't help but be a little excited and hopes that she will get a long with him. When they finally meet, Greta was not expecting him to be pierced and tattooed, or hot. Elec is a total jerk to her from the moment they are introduced. He continuously picks on Greta. Greta decides to be nice to him anyway and hopefully he'll come around. They go back and forth from getting along a little bit, to not getting along at all. This continues for quite some time until the sexual tension between them becomes too much. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You were the best thing that ever happened to me. I hope someday I can say you were <i>one</i> of the best, but for now, it's only you."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>They eventually open up to each other and understand each other better. Elec doesn't have a good relationship with his father, who verbally abuses him. Greta and Elec form a bit of a bond, and with it, the connection they share grows, too. After trying to deny what they feel, they finally share one night together. But something comes up and Elec must leave. This causes them to part and not see each other until seven years later. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413769632ra/11560530.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I really enjoyed the first part of this book. I loved Elec in the first part, especially when he became vulnerable. Plus, he has many piercings on his body. Yup, he has one down there too *grins*. I liked Greta at first, but she very soon ended up annoying me. I didn't agree with some of the things she did or thought. I liked that I was able to feel the connection between Elec and Greta. The steam was very good, but I just wish there were more scenes of it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“You make me feel things, Greta. You always have. When I’m around you, whether it’s good or bad…I feel <i>everything</i>."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I also for the most part enjoyed part two, but I did not like that we were retold part one, just in Elec's POV. I would have preferred an alternating POV throughout the book instead. Still, I'm glad I got to get inside his head. I also would have liked to have seen Greta grow up a bit. She seemed almost exactly the same in thoughts and behaviour as she did when she was a teen. I was happy that the sexual tension between them was still very present in part two. I loved the ending, I just wish we could have seen them happy together a little bit longer. Overall, it wasn't a bad read at all. I did enjoy it. It did have some flaws but it was still very good. If you want an enjoyable forbidden love story, then this one is it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412651085i/11402471._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6093295575397266993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1067600997" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10996158779857715363"><b>5 YES YES OH PLEASE YES STARS</b><br/><br/>I picked up Stepbrother Dearest for two reasons, one, it’s by Ward and two, hello, storyline! Stepbrother and stepsister, oh you know it’s going to be good.<br/><br/><b>AND IT IS GOOD</b><br/><br/>If you are looking for an emotional, intense, roller coaster read, then this one is for you. If you are looking for a jerk of a Hero you want to hate and love, then Elec is for you.<br/><br/><b>Summary</b><br/><br/>To sum it up, Elec moves in with Greta to live with her and the family for a year. Elec is mean, says off handed </span>
  <span id="freeText10996158779857715363" style="display:none"><b>5 YES YES OH PLEASE YES STARS</b><br><br>I picked up Stepbrother Dearest for two reasons, one, it’s by Ward and two, hello, storyline! Stepbrother and stepsister, oh you know it’s going to be good.<br><br><b>AND IT IS GOOD</b><br><br>If you are looking for an emotional, intense, roller coaster read, then this one is for you. If you are looking for a jerk of a Hero you want to hate and love, then Elec is for you.<br><br><b>Summary</b><br><br>To sum it up, Elec moves in with Greta to live with her and the family for a year. Elec is mean, says off handed comments to Greta and wants nothing to do with his new family. Greta is the sweet sister that tries to see past Elec’s harsh demeanor.<br><br><b>Greta and Elec</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/vsxEuHn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412730616i/11414860.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Ht99Pof" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412730648i/11414861.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What worked so well for me is simply the two main characters. Ward creates these characters that have so much depth and so much angst and so many issues, you just can’t stop reading!<br><br>And I didn’t. I read this sucker in one sitting and I could have read more.<br><br>Greta is a sweet heart. She’s the girl you want to be friends with and talk to on the phone. She tries really hard to form some friendship with Elec, but Elec makes it very different.<br><br>Ward is known to create really really really mean heroes. I’m use to this and I love it. Some of the things Elec does and says I’m just grinning from ear to ear, because it’s so mean, but it makes for such a great read.<br><br>He calls her pretty plain, he says she is pathetic and he continues to make snide remarks. It’s pretty fantastic.<br><br><b>Overall</b><br><br>I would describe the first half of the book just filled with youthful tension and banter. I love the relationship Greta and Elec have and you are just rooting for them to kiss. The second half would be more angsty and a little darker. The emotions of the two are heightening. I enjoyed both aspects of the book and couldn’t see it any other way. I felt like it really rounded the story.<br><br>The only part I couldn’t take was Elec’s POV you will get for a bit. I felt like it was a tad redundant and I understood what Ward was trying to do, but still I didn’t feel like reread again. I kind of skimmed that part.<br><br>Other that than, if you are a Ward fan and like her style of writing as I do, then you will not be disappointed. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22843341.Stepbrother_Dearest" title="Stepbrother Dearest by Penelope Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1407407844s/22843341.jpg" alt="Stepbrother Dearest by Penelope Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00NVY6JPC/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00NVY6JPC&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=GCWETZOSXFKE7SFO" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10996158779857715363" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I didn’t expect it to attempt to have a story. What I got instead was like <b>zero</b> smut and a terrible first half that had my eyes rolling so far back in my head I thought I’d never get them straightened out. But the second half was actually fairly decent . . . . minus the still no dirty sexuals for me to perv out on. Apparently I read it wrong because I took a gander at other reviews and it seems everyone hated the second half but liked the first. It’s okay, I’m used to wrongreading at this point. At least I can say I have read a "taboo" romance and I will definitely check out more stuff by this author in the future. <div id="review_1730135398" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1730135398" />
    <a title="Bibi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33411728-bibi"><img alt="Bibi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602128191p2/33411728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1730135398?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bibi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bibi" href="/user/show/33411728-bibi">Bibi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23285593-stepbrother-dearest">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1730135398" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer381083890250849100"><blockquote>
<b>Seeing I’ve had this book on my TBR list going on a year or so, I honestly can't tell you why it sat there unread.</b> <br/><br/>Indeed the gazillion 5-star reviews were compelling enough to waive my resolve and at my weakest they seemed to mock <a href='http://s1248.photobucket.com/user/bibifagboyegun/media/82c5f384-77b0-4331-8478-66f92f9d4241_zps2gucpnji.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475982556i/20789506.png' alt=' photo 82c5f384-77b0-4331-8478-66f92f9d4241_zps2gucpnji.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/>as well as attempt the much-needed kick to my derriere.<a href='http://s1248.photobucket.com/user/bibifagboyegun/media/l2Je7IxIDCIZmMtCo_zpsesjauml5.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475982556ra/20789507.gif' alt=' photo l2Je7IxIDCIZmMtCo_zpsesjauml5.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><br/>Except, previous encounters with P. Ward’s work, and the desire for my sanity, left me little choice but to continue my unintentional boycott.<br/><br/><b>The arrival of Neighbor Dearest upended the standoff. I needed to know</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText381083890250849100" style="display:none"><blockquote>
<b>Seeing I’ve had this book on my TBR list going on a year or so, I honestly can't tell you why it sat there unread.</b> <br><br>Indeed the gazillion 5-star reviews were compelling enough to waive my resolve and at my weakest they seemed to mock <a href="http://s1248.photobucket.com/user/bibifagboyegun/media/82c5f384-77b0-4331-8478-66f92f9d4241_zps2gucpnji.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475982556i/20789506.png" alt=" photo 82c5f384-77b0-4331-8478-66f92f9d4241_zps2gucpnji.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>as well as attempt the much-needed kick to my derriere.<a href="http://s1248.photobucket.com/user/bibifagboyegun/media/l2Je7IxIDCIZmMtCo_zpsesjauml5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475982556ra/20789507.gif" alt=" photo l2Je7IxIDCIZmMtCo_zpsesjauml5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>Except, previous encounters with P. Ward’s work, and the desire for my sanity, left me little choice but to continue my unintentional boycott.<br><br><b>The arrival of Neighbor Dearest upended the standoff. I needed to know who was this Elec and why had he such residual power over the female MC from ND (I don't even remember her name...that's how disinterested I am in this entire series).</b> A wise man once said: to go forward one must first go backward (was that Confucius or the Sensei from The Karate Kid?) What?!!!!! Sheesh, no need to shout. I will give you the review in a minute. Sheesh......<br><br>So, yeah. I had to first read Stepbrother Dearest before attempting ND. After reading both, I came to the realization of two things:<br><br>1. Thank fuck Ward's writing and grammar skills improved since writing SD, and<br>2. My unintentional boycott indeed was warranted<br><br>ON to the story. SD, premised on a forbidden love/taboo plot, is a story where two teenagers become pseudo-related simply as a consequence of their parents marrying each other. Let's be clear, Elec and Greta having a sexual relationship would have only made for awkward family dinners and no more. Therefore, the unnecessary angst of their love-hate relationship was a reflection, both on <b>Elec, the dim-witted-douche-bag and Greta, the collector-of-shoe-debris.</b><br><br><b>There is no story here and yet, unluckily for us, this author told the exact story twice within this book. First, from Greta's POV; then as a novel written for Greta's eyes only but narrated in Elec's words and from his POV. Confused yet? Yes. Word by word. The same story told twice (<i>with one part written entirely in italics</i>). In the same book. AM I YELLING?!!! Yes. </b><br><br>And that's because SD IMO is insanely juvenile while being utterly predictable and as it being the final straw, Ward, therefore, has earned a prime spot on my authors-to-not-read-again list.<br><br>Should this review somehow find itself lost in the sea of the many, to reach one person only, I'll consider my duty as done and will expect my wings and halo without delay!</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="381083890250849100" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4HVilStdBPXViE8It8It/6Cl/M5KB+EKE485NtdyWCeTbbnZ74Sc41olJfnWr1WlMu5s2e030sNK0adsPZ0HwA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer5385059756383518786">Penelope Ward is a New York Times, USA Today and #1 Wall Street Journal Bestselling author.<br/><br/>She grew up in Boston with five older brothers and spent most of her twenties as a television news anchor before switching to a more family-friendly career.<br/><br/>Penelope lives for reading books in the new adult genre, coffee and hanging out with her friends and family on weekends.<br/><br/>She is the proud mother of a beau</span>
  <span id="freeText5385059756383518786" style="display:none">Penelope Ward is a New York Times, USA Today and #1 Wall Street Journal Bestselling author.<br /><br />She grew up in Boston with five older brothers and spent most of her twenties as a television news anchor before switching to a more family-friendly career.<br /><br />Penelope lives for reading books in the new adult genre, coffee and hanging out with her friends and family on weekends.<br /><br />She is the proud mother of a beautiful 15-year-old girl with autism (the inspiration for the character Callie in Gemini) and a 13-year-old boy, both of whom are the lights of her life.<br /><br />Penelope, her husband and kids reside in Rhode Island.<br /><br />She is a 21-time New York Times bestseller and the author of over twenty novels.</span>
